LOI Gldl THIEU
Y hoc co truyen cung nhit y hoc hien dai la mot nganh hoc, trong 
do bao gom rat nhieu chuyen khoa. Ngoai khoa y hoc co truyen ra dcfi 
rat sdm, ke tit khi con ngitdi phai chong dd vdi thien nhien de duy tri siJt 
sinh ton va phat trien ciia minh. Theo thdi gian, chuyen nganh nay 
cang ngay cang ditOc xay ditng, cung co va hoan thien hcfn. Trong y hoc 
co truyen, quan niem ve ngoai khoa co khac vdi y hoc hien dai ngay 
nay, nhiing benh nam trong llnh viCc ngoai khoa khong chi bao gom 
nhiing benh ly phai sit dung sit can thiep ciia dao keo, bang bo, co dinh 
nhit: chan thitdng, gay xitcfng, tri... ma con bao gom ca nhitng benh 
ngoai da nhit mun nhot, benh da lieu, triing thu can... mot pham vi 
rong. De bao ton ban sac cua y hoc co truyen, sit phan loai, sap xep nay 
van ditac duy tri.
Cuon Ngoai khoa y hoc co truyen da dittic xuat ban Ian thit nhat 
nam 2002 va dd ditdc tai ban co chinh sita va bo sung Ian thit hai nam 
2006, do hai tac gia PGS. TS. Pham Van Trinh va TS. Le Litcfng Dong, 
la nhitng giang vien chinh chuyen sau ve chuyen nganh nay trong Khoa
Y hoc co truyen - Tritdng Dai hoc Y Ha Noi bien soan chinh ly. Ngoai 
khoa Y hoc co truyen nham dap iing lam tai lieu tham khao cho sinh 
vien va cac hoc vien sau dai hoc cua khoa, cung nhit lam tai lieu tham 
khao cho cac ban dong nghiep quan tam tdi llnh vitc ngoai khoa y hoc 
co truyen.
Chung tdi danh gia day la mot cuon sach co gia tri hoc tap va 
tham khao cho cac sinh vien, hoc vien va cac ban dong nghiep thuoc 
chuyen nganh y hoc co truyen. Chung tdi xin gidi thieu vdi cac ban doc 
cuon sach Ngoai khoa y hoc co truyen vdi tam long tran trong.

I. QUAN NIEM VA PHAN LOAI
Benh ngoai khoa thUc ra co rat s6m va co tru6c cac benh cua cac khoa 
khac ke ca noi khoa vi con ngUdi sinh ra phai lao dong de sinh ton cho nen 
trUdc tien phai xuat hien cac kinh nghiem dieu tri: tai nan lao dong, con 
trung va thu can... nhUng tCf xUa cac y van de lai, 6 nUdc ta chUa xep rieng 
ngoai khoa. O Trung Quoc thdi nha Chu xep do la dUdng khoa, thay thuoc 
dieu tri benh dUdng khoa goi la dUdng y.
Thdi xUa cho rang cac benh sinh ra ma mat nhin thay, tay sd thay, co 
chiing trang cuc bo deu thuoc pham vi cua ngoai khoa (vi du: dinh, ung, thu, 
hau boi, tien boi, ddn doc, loa lich, ro, nham, bif6u co...). Sau nay do khoa 
hoc phat trien va co sU ket hdp giufa y hoc co truyen v6i y hoc hien dai cho 
nen pham vi ngoai khoa rong hdn, phong phu hOn (vi du: sa lam, chan 
thUdng, con trung va thu can, cac benh da lieu, viem tac dong mach, tri...)
Trong ngoai khoa y hoc co truyen, ngUdi ta dUa vao cac benh tinh va 
nguyen nhan co the chia cac loai:
-  
Loai nhiet (thuoc loai viem nhiem theo y hoc hien dai): dinh, ung, 
thu, ddn doc, loa lich, sdi, dau v.v.
-  
Chan thUdng: triet thUdng, niu thUdng, toa thUdng, huyet ijf, khi tre 
d tang phu do chan thUdng.
-  
Cac loai khac: nham, bong (hoa sang), lanh cong (dong sang), con 
trung va thu can.
Ngoai ra diia vao y hoc hien dai ngUdi ta con chia ra cac benh theo vi tri 
ton thUdng ket hdp vcii tinh chat cua benh:
-  
Cac benh viem nhiem da, cd, xUdng, kh6p, hach va tuyen vu.
-  
Cac benh cap tinh.
-  
Cac benh hau mon - trUc trang.
-  
Cac benh da lieu.
-  
Cac benh thuoc chan thUdng.
7


-  
Cac benh u.
-  
Cac benh bong.
-  
Cac benh bi con trung va thu can.
-  
Cac benh ngoai khoa khac: soi gan, soi mat, soi tiet nieu, viem tac 
dong - tinh mach, giun chui ong mat...
II. KHAI QUAT VE BIEN CHL/NG BENH NGOAI KHOA
1. Bien chufng nguyen nhan sinh benh
Nguyen nhan gay benh ngoai khoa la do cac nguyen nhan ben ngoai (luc 
dam), cac nguyen nhan ben trong (noi nhan) va cac nguyen nhan khac (bat 
ngoai noi nhan) gay nen nhUng co dac tinh gay benh khac v6i noi khoa. Cu 
the cac nguyen nhan sau:
1.1. Nguyen nhan ben ngoai
Luc dam, ta doc con goi la ngoai cam luc dam (ttic la ngoai ta) gay nen 
(bao gom: phong, han, thu, thap, tao va hoa xam nhap vao cO the lam ton 
thUdng cO the ma phat benh). Benh co the phat tai cho (cuc bo), cung co the 
phat ra toan than la tuy thuoc vao chi'nh khi (siic de khang) cua cO the. 
Chinh khi toan than hu gay benh toan than (mun, nhot toan than); chmh 
khi tai cho hu gay benh tai cho (nhot, ung... tai cho). Benh cuc bo chiem ty le 
70 - 80%.
Nguyen nhan gay benh trong ngoai khoa thudng do hoa. Nam loai ta khi 
khac ket hop vdi hoa de gay benh, nhufng ban than chung cung bien thanh 
hoa de gay benh con goi la hoa doc hoac nhiet doc. Vi vay sach Noi kinh co 
noi: “chinh khi con ben trong, ta khi khong lam gi dUdc”.
a. Phong ta
Phong ta la dUdng ta, tinh cua phong la tao nhe, tan, len tren va ra 
ngoai, cho nen benh 6 da thudng rai rac nhieu ndi, co khi toan than, tap 
trung 6 dau, co, mat, ngiia va kho hoac co vay mong hoac te bi.
Vi du: phong xam nhap lam cho huyet tao, bi phu kem nuoi dUdng ma 
smh benh (nhu viem da than kinh, vay nen...).
Phong thich hanh (di dong) ma lai bien hoa nen phat benh nhanh va 
thay doi vi tri, hinh dang, phan nhieu thuoc diidng chiing nen xuat hien 
sifng, do, dau, khong co vi tri nhat dinh hoac len kinh giat co rut, vi du: bi 
vet thudng cam phai phong ta gay benh noi phong co the gap trong pha
8


thtfdng phong (giong nhif uon van, neu la uon van thi can phai phong va 
dieu tri bang y hoc hien dai trifdc).
b. Han ta
Han ta la am ta, tinh chat benh 0 sau, tham, te bi, benh d can xifdng, benh 
phan nhieu thuoc am chutng. Dac diem benh ngoai khoa cua han la sifng ma 
khong cijfng, mau s&c da tham tia hoac mau da trifdc khi bi benh khong do, 
khong nong, dau nhieu 0 mot vi tri nhat dinh, benh am tham va nang.
Vi du: nguyen nhan do han lam cho khi huyet if tre gay nen nhutc dau, 
chi lanh buot tai nhdt, tham chi thieu huyet nuoi difdng lam cho cd teo nho, 
rung dot tay hoac chan, gap trong benh thoat thuf (viem tac dong mach); hoac 
neu do han ta xam nhap nhieu va lau gay nen ngifng tre khi huyet lam cho 
toan than ctfng dd va lanh buot, do la benh dong thifOng (benh lanh cong).
c. Hod ta
Hoa ta thuoc difdng ta, bieu hien trieu chiing chung: ngiia, dau, Id loet... 
Tat ca deu do hoa, phong, han, thii, thap ta hoa hoa gay nen, phat benh dac 
biet nhanh va cap tinh (sifng, do, nong, dau).
Vi du: nhiet vao huyet gay nen huyet nhiet, co the gay ddn doc hoac hoa 
nhiet doc nhif: benh dinh, thu, ung, nhot... Tuy theo vi tri ma gay chiing 
benh khac nhau nhif d da la ddn doc; d cd bieu la dinh, thu, ung, nhot; d kinh 
mach nhif viem hach; d truf6c ngUc la tien boi, d sau lufng la hau boi.
Tif vi tri cua benh ma ngUdi ta co the biet cac nguyen nhan ket hdp v6i 
hoa, cu the: neu phat benh d bo phan tren cd the nhif: dau, mat, co, chi tren 
la do hoa thtfdng do hoa ket hdp v6i phong; neu d ngilc, siJdn, bung thifdng 
do hoa Lf lau, goi la hoa uat vi khi hoa thifdng uat d giiia cd the; neu phat 
benh d bo phan da6i cd the nhuf hau mon, chi dudi, sinh due, tiet nieu... thi 
thufdng la do hoa ket hdp vdi thap vi tinh chat cua thap la ha giang (di xuong 
difdi). Tuy vay khi chan doan nguyen nhan can phai ket hdp vdi trieu chufng 
toan than, tai cho va vi tri benh tren cd the de dieu tri mdi de lai ket qua tot.
d. Thap ta
Thap ta la am ta, cd tinh chat nhdt, dinh, ban due, thifdng ket hdp vdi 
han hoac nhiet tuy theo sif thien lech cua han hoac nhiet trong cd the va cua 
quy tiet (khi trdi) ma hoa han, hoa nhiet; han hoac nhiet ket hdp vdi thap 
thanh thap han, thap nhiet.
Dac diem: neu d cd (nhuc) thi da loet nat, chay nifdc hoac chay mu; d sau 
thi gay ro ri, da am ifdt (vi du: thap nhiet gap d tri, loet nat, ung thung; thap 
han gap d chi difdi nhif: cac vet loet lau lien, ro mu...).
9


e. Tao ta
Tao ta la difdng ta, dac diem cua tao la lam ton hai tan dich gay huyet 
tao sinh ra phong; do do phan nhieu benh phat d tay, chan va da (bi phu)... 
Tinh chat cua tao la bi phu kho, ne, ngiia, man, bong vay, niit ke...
Vi du: neu nhiet tao xam nhap vao huyet sinh huyet tao, huyet nhiet co 
the gap d benh vay nen; neu huyet tao co the gap benh thap chan man tinh, 
da man ngifa (nhu benh a sifng, cham).
f. Thit ta
Thii ta la difdng ta, thifdng hiep (thap), thap bi thii chifng dot lau hoa 
nhiet cho nen phan nhieu phat ra d cd, da, dau, mat. Dac diem la sifng, do, 
nung mu, dau, gap lanh cac trieu chifng giam.
Vi du: thu thap nung dot lam cho bi phu thanh rom say hoac cam phai 
thu doc thanh vet thifdng Id loet, mun nifdc (nhU: zona, dau...).
1.2. Nguyen nhan ben trong
Nguyen nhan ben trong con goi la noi thifdng that tinh, do la nhan to 
tinh than, cu the la: hi (vui), no (gian), bi (buon), ai (lo), kinh (hai), khung 
(sd), ifu (suy nghi) bi rol loan lam cho am difdng khong dieu hoa, khi huyet 
khong hoa hdp, cong nang cua cac tang phu va kinh lac bi hon loan ma gay 
benh. Benh ngoai khoa hay gap la do lo nghl hoac tCfc gian qua do. Vi du: 
tinh chi khong thong, tiic gian qua do lam cho can khi uat ket, khi tre dam 
ngifng; hay gap tren lam sang la benh viem hach (loa lich), viem tuyen vu, 
tac tia sufa, u giap trang, cac khoi u... Ngoai ra con gap cac benh ngoai da 
nhif: viem da th&n kinh, benh san ngiia... cung do yeu to'that tinh gay nen.
1.3. Cac nguyen nhan khac
a. An uong khong dieu do
Hai Thifdng Lan Ong da noi: “An uong la boi dap nhiing chat cho cho thieu, 
an uong qua mifc thi thifdng ton tdi ty vi dao trifdng”, cho nen an uong 
khong dieu do cung la nguyen nhan gay benh ngoai khoa.
Vi du: an nhieu thii cay, nong, beo, ngot, lam cho vi trifdng tich nhiet, 
hoa doc noi sinh gay nen benh Id loet, dinh, nhot, rom say...; an uong qua 
nhieu gay nen thifc tfch sinh benh cap tinh 6 bung nhif ngo thiic, viem tuy 
cap; an thiic an lanh hoac qua doi gay nen cac benh giun nhif: t&c ruot do 
giun, giun chui ong mat (hoi quyet)...
b. Phong due
Trong tap Noi kinh yeu chi Hai Thifdng Lan Ong da noi ro: “Sinh hoat la 
ky cifdng cua hanh dong... say dam ve sac goi la phong due qua do, tiu sac 
bifa bai goi la benh hao; say dam sac due qua miic thi goi la tinh can, bifa bai
10


thi tinh khi tan m an”. Nhif vay neu phong due qua do gay than khi ton 
thuong phong ta, han thap de xam nhap ma sinh benh (vi du: viem tuy 
xUdng, xifdng gay lau lien, cot trifng...).
c. Ncti d
Ndi d cung la nhan to" gay benh vi ndi 0 co lien quan chat che tdi luc dam 
va cung la yeu to" sinh ra luc dam. Vi vay benh ngoai khoa do ndi d gay nen 
chinh la do luc dam gay nen cac benh bieu hien giong nhif cac benh cua luc 
dam.
d. Cac nguyen nhan khac
-  
Chan thifdng.
-  
Con trung va thu can.
-  
Hoa thifdng va dong thifdng.
Cac ton thifdng tren neu benh nhe thi cd, da, gan, xifdng bi ton thifdng; 
neu benh nang thi cac tang phu bi ton thifdng; neu benh nghiem trong hdn 
thi bien benh toan than.
2. Bien chufng va benh ly
Benh ly la mot khai niem hieu biet ve benh, giai thfch difdc nguyen nhan 
gay benh trong cd the va phan tich difdc sii bien hoa cua benh, danh gia tien 
lifdng cua benh, cho nen no het sifc quan trong. Tren thifc te lam sang, no cd y 
nghia chi dao trong yeu trong chan doan, dieu tri, phong va tien lifdng benh.
2.1. Bien chiing ve khi huyet
Khi huyet trong cd the giup dd lan nhau ma lifu hanh, tuan hoan trong 
kinh mach, d trong thi nuoi difdng tang phu, d ngoai thi nuoi difdng cd da de 
duy tri sU song va cd tac dung chong ngoai ta xam nhap. Vi vay khi huyet 
vUdng thinh, sif bao ve ben ngoai se manh thi ngoai ta khong de xam nhap; 
khi huyet hif yeu, sU bao ve ben ngoai se kem thi cac nguyen nhan gay benh 
rat de xam nhap ma gay nen benh. Sach Noi kinh ndi: "Khi thifdng thi dau, 
hinh (huyet) thifdng thi sifng. Sifng va dau la phan ting benh ly khong giong 
nhau cua hai loai khi va huyet bi ngifng tre”. Vi vay phat sinh ra ton thifdng 
benh ly ngoai khoa nhat thiet phai do khi huyet ngu'ng tre gay nen.
Vi du trong ngoai khoa chan thifdng: khi huyet ngifng tre la nguyen 
nhan chu yeu phat sinh va hinh thanh benh ly sifng nong do dau hoac chay 
mau (vi du benh Id loet, dinh, nhot...); neu khi huyet xung thinh (du) thi d 
thdi ky dau de dang khoi, d thdi ky cd mu de thu nho va vd mu, d thdi ky vd 
mu de thu nho mieng vet thifdng va sinh cd (lien seo).
11


Vi vay khi bien chiing trong lam sang nhat thiet phai lam ro quan he khi 
huyet vdi benh noi ton thifdng m6i hieu difdc ban chat cua benh ma tien 
hanh dinh ra phUdng hu6ng dieu tri. Cac bieu hien cua ton thifdng khi huyet 
nhif sau:
a. Khi tre
Khi tu thi co hinh, khi tan thi khong co vet tich, khi gay benh thi dau, 
khi dau thi bat thudng. Benh thifdng gap nhif: ngifc sifdn day t\jfc, kho thd do 
chan thudng vao ngifc sifdn (khong co trieu chifng gay xifdng, tran khi, tran 
dich mang phoi, khong vd gan lach); hoac loi keo gay dau; hoac danh nhau 
vimg bung gay tiic bung, chifdng hdi; hoac lun gay cot song gay chifdng 
bung, bi dai tieu tien; hoac cung co the do tang phu bi roi loan gay khi tre 
nhif benh khi hif ha ham (sa cac phu tang...)
b. Khi uat
Khi uat trong ngoai khoa co the sinh ra tich tu; hoac khi uat hoa hoa, 
hoa dot chay tan dich ma thanh ddm, ddm tich lai thanh khoi. Neu khi uat 
ma tich tu, thanh khoi, mau sac da khong thay doi, co the thay doi theo tinh 
chi (vi du: viem tuyen vu, tac tia sufa, u giap trang...); neu khi uat hoa hoa, 
hoa dot chay tan dich thanh dam, dam se tich lai thanh khoi sifng nhUng 
mem (vi du: viem hach man...).
c. Khi hit
Khi hif tiic la difdng khi khong the thong dat cd bieu vao ben trong cd the 
difdc. Neu khi hif toan than gay cif dong kho khan, hay gap trong di chiing 
cua cac chan thifdng than kinh, cd, xifdng, kh6p... Neu khi hif tai cho thi siic 
chong dd tai cho yeu cho nen doc ta de xam nhap gay ra 16 loet, dinh, nhot... 
lam cho cac ndi bi ton thifdng kho hoi phuc (vi du: benh khi hif cua tang phu 
nhu ty khi hif gay nen sa cac phu tang). Neu khi hif ca tai cho va toan than 
nhu benh sifng mu thi kho pha mu, kho thu mieng, thd yeu, an kem, chat 
lifdi nhdt, mach te.
d. Huyet it
Theo y hoc co truyen: trong ngoai khoa ‘Thifdng khi tkc khi tre, thifdng 
huyet t^c huyet ngifng”. Khi tre khien huyet ngifng, huyet ngifng thi can trd 
khi hanh, vi vay huyet if la gay ra benh. Neu huyet ii ngifng d cd nhuc, bi 
phu thi sifng, dau, do (vi du: ton thifdng cd, da, day ch^ng - ton thifdng ph^n 
mem); neu can trd d dinh ve thi uat ma sinh nhiet, benh co trieu chiing 
sifng, nong, do, dau d da, cd (vi du: benh dinh, nhot, loet...); neu huyet tich d 
ngiic sifdn thi co trieu chiing day chifdng, dau, tiic d ngifc sifdn (vi du: benh 
viem difdng mat, ton thifdng viing ngiic do chan thifdng).
12


Huyet ii lau uat thanh nhiet (noi d phan difdi), huyet 
cung gay ra chay 
mau (vi du: tri chay mau).
e. Huyet nhiet
Huyet nhiet do huyet H lau, uat d trong ma sinh nhiet hoac nhiet doc 
xam pham vao huyet phan. Neu d da, cd, kh6p... thi co trieu chiing nhiet cap 
tinh nhif: sifng, nong, do, dau; gap trong dinh, ddn doc, nhot... do la do huyet 
lau uat thanh nhiet gay nen. Neu co trieu chiing chay mau thi do nhiet 
vao huyet nen biic huyet loan hanh ma gay ra; thifdng gap trong tho huyet, 
nuc huyet, do sang chan...
f. Huyet hit
Huyet hif thifdng xuat hien d thdi ky sau cua benh. Y hoc co truyen cho 
r^ng khi huf bat dung, huyet hif bat nhan, cho nen cac ndi ton thifdng ma 
huyet hif thi khong nuoi difdng difdc, do vay ndi ton thifdng se teo cd, ciing 
can kho hoi phuc van dong (vi du: cac vet thifdng ma huyet hif thi rat kho 
thu mieng va lien seo hoac trong cac trifdng hdp gay xifdng neu huyet hif thi 
se kho lien xifdng...).
2.2. Bien chiing ve can xUdng
Can lien quan t6i can, xifdng lien quan t6i than, can va xifdng la ngon 
cua can than, difdc khi huyet on am va can than nhu difdng. Vi vay can 
xifdng ma bi ton thifdng thi nhat thiet ton thifdng t6i khi huyet va anh 
hifdng t6i can than.
Nhiing ngifdi tre tuoi (nhat la liia tuoi thanh nien) co can than khi thinh, 
can xifdng phat trien ch&c cho nen can xifdng bi ton thifdng thi rat de hoi 
phuc. Ngifdi gia thi can than khi suy, can xifdng hif yeu cho nen can xifdng bi 
ton thifdng thi hoi phuc rat cham, tham chi khong hoi phuc. Vi vay, dieu tri 
benh can xifdng can phai chu y den dieu ly cua khi huyet can than lam chu.
Vi du: gay xifdng giai doan dau con sifng, nong, do, dau thi can hoat 
huyet, hanh khi, tieu ii lam chu; den giai doan het sifng, nong, do phai chu y 
lam lien xifdng, lay bo can than lam chu...
2.3. Bien chiing ve tang phu
Trong ngoai khoa benh co quan he chat che vdi tang phu. Benh co the tif 
bieu truyen vao tang phu (vi du: cac benh ngoai da, cd, can, xifdng tuy do 
ngoai ta gay benh nhifng neu khong dieu tri tot se gay benh d tang phu nhif 
dinh, nhot; neu ngifdi benh co chinh khi kem se gay sot cao, hoa mu toan 
than va co giat difa den txi vong...); ngifdc lai benh thuoc tang phu cung co

Cac benh d da, cd, xifdng, khdp du chan thifdng hay cac doc ta gay nen 
deu lam khi huyet t&c trd gay nen khi huyet d kinh lac ngifng tre, do vay

a. Sitng
Trong cd the ngifdi ta khi huyet tuan hanh khong ngifng, khong ndi nao 
khong den, khong ndi nao khong qua. Neu do nguyen nhan nao do lam khi 
huyet dong lai hoac ngifng tre thi tai ndi do co sifng dau. Hinh thai cung 
nhif mau sac d moi cho sifng deu khac nhau: cho sifng tan man thuoc hif; 
cho sifng cao, tap trung thuoc thiic; sifng thuoc phong thi cho sifng noi 
phong ma hay chay; sifng thuoc dam thi mem nhun nhif bong hoac ngoai 
ciing trong mem khong do, khong nong, mau da nhif thifdng. Vi il huyet ma 
sifng thi sac hdi hong hong hoac bam tim. Neu thanh mu thi mau sac bien 
doi (co the tim bam lan vang, hoac mau xanh); sifng do huyet khong chay; 
sifng do khi thi chay.
b. Dau
Dau chinh la do khi khong lifu thong nhifng khi la thong soai cua 
huyet, huyet la me cua khi nen khi khong lifu thong thi huyet cung khong 
lifu thong, cho nen ngifdi ta noi r&ng dau la do khi huyet khong lifu thong 
va cung tuy theo nguyen nhan ma co tinh chat dau khac nhau. Neu dau 
thuoc hif thi ifa xoa bop, gap lanh lai dau tang; dau thuoc han thi tu lai 
mot cho, mau da khong thay doi, gap nong thi b6t dau; dau thuoc nhiet thi 
mau hong do, gap lanh thi dau giam; vi lam mu ma dau thi vufa dau vifa 
sifng to, vi phong ma dau thi dau chay khap ngifdi rat nhanh, kem theo 
ngiia, te bi hoac kien can; vi khi ma dau thi dau chay quanh khong nhat 
dinh cho nao.

c. Lam mu

day doc ra ngoai dUdc. Vi the ngifdi ta noi rang stf bai nung cac chiing ung 
nhot, sang ung... la do chinh khi day doc ra ngoai, lam cho doc theo mu ra 
ngoai, cho nen benh lam mu nhif ung, nhot, thung, doc da den giai doan 
thanh hinh thi phai kham xet ky xem da lam mu chifa, mu 6 sau hay nong 
de xii ly cho dung; hoac neu co mu thi da v6 chifa va xem xet tinh chat, mui, 
mau cua mu.
PhUdng phap kham nhot mu: lay hai ngon tay an nhe ndi sifng, neu thay 
bap benh la co mu, co ntfdc; an vao thay Cling ran la chifa co mu, mem nhun 
d trong la co mu da chin; an nhe thay dau ngay la co mu d nong, an nang

khong thay doi lai khong co len la mu d sau.

huyet hif yeu thi mu ra loang va trang. Neu mu ra nhif nifdc due .hoac nifdc 
bot (neu la nifdc mu thoi), do la chiing chiia difOc. Neu luc dau ra mu vang

thifdng, de thu mieng va len da non. Neu sac mu nhif dau trau hoac chay nifdc 
vang (hoac nifdc trong) thudng nam trong chiing chiia lau va kho.
d. NgiCa

Phiidng phap dieu tri benh ngoai khoa bao gom dieu tri ben trong (noi 
tri) va dieu tri ben ngoai (ngoai tri). Dieu tri ben trong la dieu tri toan than, 
dieu tri ben ngoai la dieu tri tai cho (cuc bo). Hai loai dieu tri nay thtfdng 
thtfdng phoi hdp vdi nhau nhiing neu benh nhe ngtfdi benh khoe thi lay dieu 
tri tai cho la chmh, neu benh nang thi nhat thiet phai ket hdp dieu tri toan 
than ket hdp dieu tri cuc bo.

tinh trang cua benh nhan, nguyen nhan gay benh, nhiing yeu to" anh htfdng 
tdi ngtfdi benh va biet dac diem khong giong nhau trong ttfng giai doan cua 
benh thi mdi mang lai hieu qua trong dieu tri.

I. OAICI/ONG
Soi tiet nieu bao gom co soi than, soi nieu quan, soi bang quang va soi 
nieu dao.
Y hoc co truyen goi soi tiet nieu la sa lam, thach lam hoac cat lam.
Soi tiet nieu gap 6 tat ca cac ltia tuoi, theo Rev frat (1976) soi tre em 
chiem 50% trtfdc 5 tuoi va 30% trtfdc 3 tuoi. Soi tiet nieu co tmh chat dia 
phtfOng nhtf chau A, chau Phi con chau Au giam ro ret. 0  Viet Nam mien 
Trung du hay gap hon 6 vung dong b&ng. O Trung Quoc vung Quang Dong, 
Ho Nam hay gap hon.

nguyen nhan da biet ro rang con mot so" chtfa biet ro cho nen van de dieu tri 
vln chtfa co phtfOng phap dieu tri dac hieu nhat la loai soi oxalat ma Viet

TRI
Tri la mot benh man tinh do cac tinh mach triic trang hau mon bi gian 
va sung huyet thanh mot bui hoac nhieu bui, tuy vi tri tinh mach d tnic trang 
hay hau mon diidc phan chia tren lam sang thanh tri noi hay tri ngoai.
Nguyen nhan gay ra tri bao gom: viem dai trang man tinh gay tao bon 
thifdng xuyen dai tien ran nhieu; viem gan, xd gan man tinh gay sung huyet 
tinh mach; cac benh nghe nghiep do diing lau hoac cd thai lam trifOng liic cd 
thanh bung va thanh tinh mach bi giam gay gian tinh mach v.v...
Vi sung huyet de gay thoat quan, chay mau, lam cho ngifdi benh thieu 
mau, boi nhiem nen ngifdi benh cd trieu chifng nhilm khuan. Tren lam sang 
can cif vao tinh trang cac bui tri, xuat huyet va nhilm khuan de phan loai 
the benh va cach chiia.
Cac giai doan cua tri noi va tri ngoai difdc phan chia nhii sau:
Tri noi: chia lam 4 thdi ky:
1. Bui tri chiia ra ngoai, dai tien ra mau tiidi, cd trifdng hdp chay mau 
nhieu gay thieu mau.
2. Khi dai tien bui tri ldi ra, sau dd tri lai co diidc.

3. Khi dai tien bui tri loi ra, di xong khong tii co len diidc.
4. Bui tri sa ra ngoai, sau dai tien phai dung tay day len nhiing khi lao 
dong nang, ngoi som lai sa xuong (thiidng kem theo sa tnic trang).
Tri ngoai: nam d ria hau mon, dUdc phu bdi da hau mon; mat do thiidng 
ran (do viem tac, huyet khoi tinh mach). Hau het benh nhan bi tri ngoai 
thudng den kham trong tinh trang viem cap tinh, huyet tac, huyet khoi tinh 
mach vdi trieu chiing noi bat la dau dii doi, kem theo cuc ran canh hau mon.
Phiidng phap chiia benh tri cd hai loai: dung thuoc uong de chong chay 
mau, chong nhiem khuan, lam nho bui tri; dung thuoc va cac thu thuat 
ngoai khoa de gay hoai tuf bui tri, rung va cat cac bui tri, loai bo huyet khoi.

GAY Xl/ONG
I. OjNH NGHlA
Gay xiidng la sii pha huy dot ngot cac cau true ben trong cua xiidng do 
nguyen nhan cd hoc. Do do gay ra sii gian doan ve truyen lilc qua xiidng.
II. NGUYEN NHAN
Hau het cac gay xiidng la do chan thiidng, do life uon be, xoan van hoac 
ca hai triic tiep hoac gian tiep gay nen. Neu mot xiidng co benh (viem, u...)bi 
gay diidc goi la gay xiidng benh ly hay con goi la gay xiidng tii nhien. Ngoai 
ra cac chan thiidng gay nhe, nhiing lap di lap lai nhieu lan gay gay xiidng 
diidc goi la gay xilOng do stress.
Ngoai gay dien hinh, d tre em thiidng gap d loai gay canh tildi, gay xiidng 
cong tao hinh, gay bong sun tiep, d ngildi cao tuoi, phu mi man kinh gay lun, 
gay cd xilOng dui, gay dau dildi xiidng quay...
Xiidng co the gay khong hoan toan: cong tao hinh, phinh vo xiidng, gay 
canh tildi, gay hoan toan lam hai hay nhieu doan, nhieu manh. Ngoai ra con 
co cac loai gay cai, gay lun, bong sun tiep hop...
Cac loai di lech dien hinh: ben-ben, gian cach hai mat gay, gap goc, va xoay.
III. BIEN CHlTNG

chiing chen ep khoang; thiidng ton mach mau 16n, than kinh ngoai bien; gay 
hd na nhiem trung, hoi chiing doi loan dinh difOng.

a. Lien xiidng trite tiep
Lane (1914) phat hien co stf lien xtfdng thing ttf mo xtfdng do mau tao 
ra. Mo xtfdng chi phat trien d ben trong khe gitfa cac mat xtfOng gay, khong 
co can bic cau. Tren phim X quang: it co hinh anh cac dtfdng can ben ngoai, 
dtfdng gay hep dan va bien mat.
De tao dieu kien cho xtfdng gay lien trtfc tiep, co trtfdng phai chu trtfdng co" 
dinh xtfdng gay ctfng, chac nhtf Kuntcher (1939); ket hdp xtfdng cua 
nhom A. 0  (1969).
Danis (1947) va nhieu tac gia thuoc nhom nghien ctfu ket hdp xtfdng 
A.O Thuy Si da co cong de xuat ra phtfdng thtfc thtfc hien cho lien xtfdng 
trtfc tiep bing bien phap tao ltfc nen ep gitfa cac mat gay va coi do la tieu 
chuan cua cac phtfdng phap ket hdp xtfdng hien dai.
Dieu kien quan trong nhat de co lien xtfdng trtfc tiep la:

con mot di dong nao gitfa hai dau gay (nhat la nhtfng di dong co hai 
nhtf di dong xoin van, uon be, di lech ngang), chi cho phep di lech 
nho theo true ty nen (di lech htfu ich la tang stf tiep xuc gitfa hai 
mat gay).

Ngoai ra, cac dieu kien khac nhtf la: dam bao ltfu thong mau nuoi 
dtfdng day du 6 vung gay, hai mat gay cang ap sat nhau cang tot.
Ve mat cO hoc, Steinmann mo ta:" Co" dinh bang tac dong cua ltfc ep ap 
chat cac mat gay xtfdng ciing va cac manh cai, nhd do tranh dtfOc bat ky cac 
di dong nao cua manh gay”.

stfa chtfa mot so" bien dang ttfdng doi tot. Ben canh do cung con nhtfng di

Ttf khai thien lap dia, Y hoc phtfOng dong da doi dau v6i dieu tri chan

Ngtfdi nguyen thuy con an song, 0 lo, khi di kiem an thtfOng dung

1. Trung y
Ttf ddi nha Chu (1066 - 255 trtfdc cong nguyen) den nha Tan 
(306 - 207 trtfdc cong nguyen) la thoi ky da co van ttf kha van minh, ngtfdi ta 
da biet dat mot che do ve y, dtfdc. Ve y co chia ra bon loai thay thuoc la thtfc 
y, tat y, dtfdng y (chtfa nhot) va thu y. Dtfdng y con chtfa ca dam chem, 
nga gay xtfOng....
Ttf ddi nha Han (206-25 trtfdc cong nguyen) den ddi nha Tan (265-420) 
mdi co mot so" sach trong do co danh rieng mot thien noi ve chan thtfdng.
Ttf ddi nha Dtfdng (608-917), ngtfdi ta dtfa khoa xtfOng gop vao khoa xoa 
bop (vi chtfa gay xtfOng cung phai sd nan, xoa, bop...).
Den ddi nha Thanh (1616-1911), vi luon luon co chien tranh, nen khoa 
xtfdng dtfOc chu y dac biet. Nam Can Long thtf nhat (1737) co trieu tap cac 
danh y trong ntfdc ban bac bien soan cuon Chinh cot phap trong do co noi ve 
nguyen nhan, trieu chtfng, cach kham, cach dieu tri gay xtfOng, sai khdp.
Ve thuoc co chia ra thuoc uong trong de giao thong huyet mach va chong 
stfng dau; thuoc dung ngoai de bo va co" dinh.
Cac loai dung cu de bo xtfOng gom:
-  True liem (cai manh manh) de co" dinh xtfOng dai.
-  Lam ly (cai giat thtfa) de co" dinh xtfdng cing tay, ckng chan.
-  Moc thong (mieng go dem vao ltfng) de co" dinh xtfOng song.
-  Yen tru ( cai dem ltfng).

Bao tat (dem bao) de co" dinh dau go"i.
2. Y hoc cd truyen Viet Nam

1. T rung Quoc (trtfdc 1964)
Tat ca cac benh vien deu ket hdp Trung Tay y trong dieu tri gay xtfdng

1.1. PliilOng phap nan bo, dung cu
Trtfdc khi nan b6 bao gid cung phai tiem te, d tre em thi phai gay me.
Dat chi d ttf the trung binh sinh ly (cd d trang thai chiing gian nhat), 
dung ltfc keo va ltfc keo ngtfdc lai, giai quyet di lech chong, di lech gap goc, di

Dung cu bo tuy khac nhau ve chat lieu d moi benh vien: nep tre nho cho

da mong cho em (Thien tan ), nhtfng deu dai gitf toan bo xtfdng hoac chdm 
khdp, cho phep khdp co the cii dong dtfdc mot phan. Ngoai viec dat nep, dem 
cung gitf mot vai trd quan trong nhim chong di lech thtf phat. Dem dtfdc lam 
bing giay ban tot, cd nhieu hinh dang khac nhau phu hdp vdi ndi dem. Vi tri 
dat dem tuy thuoc cd che di lech va nhiem vu co" dinh.
1.2. Ket qua dieu tri
Phtfdng phap dieu tri tren da dtfdc ap dung cho tren 16000 trtfdng hdp 
gay kin than xtfOng d moi ltfa tuoi, tren nhieu loai gay, ke ca loai gay kho 
nhtf gay than xtfOng dui 0 ngtfdi ldn, gay co chan kem trat khdp chay sen. 
Trong so 40 benh nhan nim dieu tri noi tru tai Benh vien Thien Tan, chi cd

ba triidng hdp md (hai vi gay xifdng dui, mot vi gay hd cing chan). So con lai 
difOc dieu tri bang phUOng phap ket hdp Trung - Tay y.
C) tat ca cac benh vien da ket hdp dieu tri, cac bac si deu nhan dinh:

CHAN THl/ONG CAC NGON TAY- BAN TAY
Gay xtfdng va trat khdp cac xtfdng ban va dot ngon tay thtfdng gap trdng 
sinh hoat hang ngay, do nhieu nguyen nhan nhtf tai nan giao thong, tai nan 
the due the thao. Vi la xtfdng nho nen nhieu ngtfdi cho la gay nhe., khong chu 
y dieu tri can than. Vi vay hau qua la nhieu trtfdng hdp mat chiic nang sau 
khi dieu tri.
Nguyen tac dieu tri:
-  
Nam vCifng giai phau vung ban tay, ngon tay, chu y ndi bam va chtic 
nang cua cac cd.

Chu trong phuc hoi hinh dang giai phau: true cac xtfdng ban, true 
ngon, do dai cac ngon va dau bup cac ngon.

Bat dong trong ttf the cd nang cua ban tay khi ban tay nghi hoan 
toan: ban tay "cam but".

Chi bat dong ngon bi ton thtfdng, tranh lam han che van dong cua 
cac ngon con lai.

loan dinh dtfdng neu bat dong lau.

I. GAY CAC XI/ONG BAN TAY
A. GAY NEN CAC XI/ONG BAN
1. Gay nen xtfOng ban I
Thtfdng gap dd nga chong tay vdi ngon cai gap tot da vao gan tay (kieu 
gay cua cac vo si quyen anh (boxer)). Can phan biet hai loai:
-  
Gay ngoai khdp.

1.1. Trieu chiing lam sang
-  
Stfng ne vung khdp thang - ban.

-  Dau choi d nen xUdng ban I, co the sd difdc dau gay nham nhd hoac 
dinh gap goc.
-  Don doc true ngon cai dau tang.

1.2. Trieu chiing X  quang
Binh thudng ngon cai nam mot ben so vdi cac ngon kia nen tren phim 
thang thay ngon nay d binh dien nghieng va ngUdc lai, tranh nham la di lech 
xoay. Phim X quang cho biet vi tri, dudng gay va di lech. Can chu y tim di 
lech gap goc.
Gay trat Bennett: dudng gay thudng la chec tii phia trUdc trong cua nen 
xifdng ban xuong khdp thang - ban, lam trat khdp xUdng ban di lech len tren, 
phia ngoai xUdng thang. Chu y xem manh gay con lai ldn hay nho.
1.3. Dieu tri
Co the dieu tri bao ton: nan bo nep to ban cang ban tay, ngon I d tu the 
dang va doi chieu (tu the nam gon qua bong tennis trong long ban tay). Neu 
co di lech, trUdc khi bo bot can phai nan siia (chu y nan gap goc bang keo 
theo true ngon tay cai day vao dinh gap goc).
Chup X quang kiem tra, gitf nep 6 tuan.
Doi vdi gay trat Bennett, nan kho khan hdn vi phai keo ngon cai cho het 
di lech chong trudc khi nan vao khdp. Dat dem ti nen vao nen dot nham 
khong cho trat lai.
Kiem tra neu cdn di lech, nan lai ngay lan hai, neu khong thanh cong 
thi chuyen dieu tri phau thuat.
2. Gay nen cac xufcfng ban I I —V
Cac gay xUdng nay thudng ft di lech. Tren lam sang chi thay sUng, an 
dau choi, don doc true lam dau tang. Chup X quang xac dinh to’n thudng.

GAY XlfONG VUNG GOI
Trong hoat dong thiidng ngay cung nhu trong luyen tap the due the 
thao, thao di§n quan sii, thi dau the thao, con ngUdi co phan xa ttf nhien 
chong dd lai stf mat thang bang cua cd the. Dau gdi thudng chiu stf va dap 
trtfc tiep lam gay xUdng dui, banh che, mam chay cang chan, dtft day chang 
cung mot luc, tao ra hinh thai gay xtfdng vung gdi rat nang goi la "goi bap 
benh" (gay ca xUdng dui, ca xUdng cang chan).
Trong trtfdng hdp dau, xac suat gay xtfdng vung gdi it hdn la ton thtfdng 
day chang. Chan thtfdng trtfc tiep tad gay xtfdng nhieu hdn ton thtfdng day 
chlng hoac ton thtfdng ca xtfdng va day chlng vung gdi. Nguyen nhan chinh 
thtfdng la tai nan giao thong gitfa xe gan may hai banh, hoac xe oto va 
xe gan may.
Tuy theo liic va cham, co the gay banh che do liic nhe hoac nga quy goi, 
Neu ltfc va cham manh co the gay mam chay, dtft day chang cheo. Liic manh 
hdn ntfa ca xUdng dui, xUdng banh che va xtfdng chay cung gay; co the kerr 
dtft day chlng cheo, vd sun chem. Trtfdng hdp "gdi bap benh", co the dan t6 
soc nguy hiem den tmh mang ngUdi bi thudng.
Ton thudng mach mau khoeo.
Long khdp sau nay.
Tuy hudng tac dong len loi cau xtfdng dui hoac mam chay ma gay ca< 
kieu gay khac nhau.
I. GAY XUONG BANH CHE
Gay xUdng banh che do chan thtfdng trtfc tiep thudng la gay hd, doi kh 
co the nhan biet tren lam sang: vd xtfdng banh che, chay dich kh6p, mai 
khong dong; khi day ch&ng canh ben xtfdng banh che bi rach (dtft) thi ha

VA NGOAI
Ton thifdng sun chem rat phiic tap can co nhiing test (nghiem phap) dac

khcip goi - (test Mac Murray, test Steinmann) ton thUdng day chlng cheo 
can chiing minh bing test ngan keo tru6c va ngan keo sau (test Slocum

IV. GAY VUNG GOI DANG GOI BAP BENH (Floating Knee)
Goi bap benh gap trong trUdng hdp gay xtfdng dui d 1/3 du6i, gay loi cau 
kem theo co gay mam chay hoac gay 1/3 tren xtfdng chay. Ldi cau xUdng dui

va mam chay deu la xtfdng xop, c6 rat nhieu mau nuoi. Khi gay xUdng dong 
mach chic chin se bi thtfdng, roi loan dong mau, de bi tic mach do md.
Ton thtfdng mach mau thtfdng xuyen co mat: can can thiep phau thuat 
kip thdi va bat dong xtfdng, ddi hoi dung cu ket hdp xUdng chuyen biet, dieu 
tri bao ton cac trtfdng hdp nay thudng it cong hieu.
Ve dieu tri, gay xtfdng banh che it bien chtfng va ft de lai di chtfng chtfc

goi sdm trd lai nhd vat ly tri lieu. Gay kieu goi bap benh, neu co soc can dieu 
tri on dinh, roi ket hdp xUdng de chtfc nang goi sdm dUdc bao toan phan nao. 
Phuc hoi chtfc nang goi doi hoi mot thdi gian dai tap luyen tap tich ctfc 
(6 - 12 thang), tuy nhien ty le phuc hoi tot chi dat < 40%. Neu goi bap benh co

goi se mat chtfc nang.

CAC GAY XI/ONG VUNG CO CHAN VA BAN CHAN
I. GAY XUONG HAI MAT CA
1. Dinh nghia
Gay hai mat ca la gay dau dudi xUdng mac (7cm cuoi) va mau tram chay 
(5cm cuoi) kem theo co hoac khong dtft day chlng chay mac dtfdi - Volkm ann 
1952 da them vao danh ttf thtf 3 cho gay mat ca la gay xUdng bd sau cua 
mat khdp chay sen.
2. Cd che gay cac mat ca
Dua tren giai phau hoc va cd che sinh hoc cua vung co chan Lauge 
Hansen (1936) da chtfng nghiem cd che gay hai mat ca thanh 4 kieu 
gay chmh:
a. Gay mat ca kieu lat ngtfa - xoay ngoai ban chan (68,5%).
b. Gay m lt ca kieu lat sap - xoay ngoai (8,5%) (con goi la kieu 
xoay ngoai).
c. Gay mat ca kieu lat sap - dang (6%).
Nim dtfdc cd che gay de nan chinh xtfdng gay phuc hoi giai phau; co 
dinh o gay vtfng vang, nhanh gon. Stf phan loai giup chung ta de ghi nhd cd 
che dac hieu cua moi kieu gay. Trong moi kieu co cac ton thudng dac hieu,
224


khong nen chi xet ton thifdng va di lech tren phim X quang, ma can suy luan 
ton thuong phan mem, de nang cao hieu qua dieu tri.
3. Nguyen nhan
Thong thudng gay hai mat ca do cd che gian tiep nhu trUdt chan, nga bi 
don ep, uon be, van xoan hoac keo cang day chang vUdt qua mUc chiu dung 
binh thUdng cua co chan. Trong thuc te thudng tai nan xay ra nhanh nen cac 
cd che co phoi hdp vdi nhau cung luc.
Nguyen nhan trUc tiep, cd che trUc tiep: chi thay trong cac trUdng hdp bi 
can dap co chan, dap co chan trUc tiep vao vat cUng hoac ngUdc lai (2 - 4%).
4. Trieu chting
Gay hai mat ca rat dau khien cho ngUdi benh khong the cii dong du'dc co 
chan ban chan va cac ngon chan. NgUdi benh co the rat dau ddn.
Vong chan: co chan bi rong ra (sau khi cdi het giay, tat d chan ra), veo 
trong neu gay mat ca ngoai, veo ngoai neu gay mat ca trong, ban chan d tu 
the buong duoi, got nho ra sau neu co trat khdp chay sen hoac gay mat ca 
thU ba di lech, sUng ne bam tim lan ndi o gay, ndi day chang bi sUt, dUt, xuat 
hien muon.
Sd cUu: nin lai tu the chung cua co chan va dat trong mang go lot em. 
Co chan, ban chan thing goc vdi mat phang chan trdi. Co the sii dung chan 
bong, goi hdi, nem bat dong tam de benh nhan bdt dau.
Van chan: dau nhieu, nhat la diem dau d giUa (trudc) co chan va doc len 
tren mat ca ngoai, chUng to cd ton thudng day chang chay mac dudi hoac 
mang lien cot. Trong trUdng hdp nay cac tac gia ldn khuyen chung ta nen 
chfch te o gay va o khdp co’ chan.
Van chan: hanh chinh, thdi gian, cd che nga.
Thiet chan: kiem tra mach co chan, ngoai trU gay mat ca kieu dudi day 
chang chay mac hoac o gay chua di lech, con cac kieu gay khac deu lam co 
chan sUng ldn. Mach mu ban chan yeu hdn vi sung to do di lech cua o gay va 
trat khdp co chan. Ep hai mat ca nhe nhang, nam cang chan va ban chan lac 
ngang thay co chan long.
Chup X quang d tu the dUng va can thiet de thay ro di lech cua xUdng 
ma suy ra ton thudng phan mem de phan loai dung dan hdn.

-  Xuyen kim, neo mat ca trong, mat ca ngoai o gay khong ton thtfdng 
day chang.
-  
Bit oc tat ca cac manh xtfdng gay va nep oc vtfng chac co dan hoi 
cua nep oc tren xtfdng mac la quan trong.
-  Khau lai tat ca cac day chlng bi dtft, stft, toac doc.
Sau phau thuat muon co ket qua tot cua kh6p cd chan, gay hai mat ca 
thi van dong s6m cd chan co vai tro quan trong.
II. GAY XI/ONG SEN, GOT, BAN VA NGON CHAN
A. CAU TRUC CHUNG CUA BAN CHAN VA CO SINH HOC
Cac xtfdng ban chan dtfdc sap xep theo phtfdng thtfc da tang thdi La Ma 
thanh hai khung doc va khung ngang, tao thanh hinh vom tam giac xtfdng 
got, chom xtfdng ban V-l, cac vom ay dtfdc vi nhtf cac canh cung va day 
chlng cd ngan long ban chan nhtf day cung co stfc dan hoi. Cac cd clng 
chan dieu khien gap duoi cd chan, lat sap - ngiia ban chan. Tuy theo ttf 
the ban chan khi rdi xuong ttf cao hay thap, stf giam da rdi nhd cac cung 
vom va day chlng lien xtfdng, cd ngln long ban chan dam nhan. Stf ham 
da do neu qua stfc chiu dtfng cua day cung thi xtfOng se gay, bong, dtft 
day chang, cd long ban chan cung bi ton thtfdng. Xtfdng nao gay tuy theo 
diem cham cua ban chan:
1. Ttf the ban chan gap ltfng toi da
a. Diem cham la xtfOng got thi xtfdng got vd trtfdc.
b. Neu diem cham la xtfdng ban thi xtfdng sen vd trtfdc, ke do la xtfdng 
ban, xtfdng nem, xtfdng hop, xtfOng ban nguyet.
Diem tap trung stfc doi van la xtfdng got.
2. Ttf the ban chan phang cham  deu tren m at ctfng
Phau thuat co nhieu cach:
232


a. Neu diem cham chiu deu len ban chan thi trong ltfdng cd the phan 
phoi tren xtfdng sen got nhieu hdn lam "lun xtfdng got" gay lun, gay xep. Vi 
xtfdng sen, got deu xop, day ch&ng got thuyen de bi ton thtfdng.
b. Chan thtfdng bd ngoai xtfdng (xtfdng ban V) ban chan chiu stfc nhieu, 
cham dat trtfdc nen xtfdng ban V gay trtfdc xtfdng ban khac vi no la dinh 
xtfdng ngoai.
3. Ttf the ban chan duoi (gap long)
Diem cham d cac dau xtfdng ban, stfc rdi dtfdc chuyen ra sau va tap 
trung vao xtfdng sen, got. Co xtfdng sen gay trtfdc va xtfdng got gay sau. Gay 
nhieu manh ldn khi ban chan trd nen gap ltfng toi da de ham da rdi.
4. Neu ttf the co ban chan bi ket trong mot chieu nhat dinh thi xtfdng sen 
va chay bi vd
a. Co chan duoi: xtfdng sen vd than sau; xtfdng chay vd nhieu manh va 
trat xtfdng sen ra trtfdc.
b. Co chan gap:
-  Gay co va than trtfdc xtfdng sen.
-  Gay bd sau dau dtfdi xtfdng chay.
B. NGUYEN NHAN
1. Chan thtfdng nhe gian tiep
Lat ban chan, trtfdt bac tam cap, xtfdng ban V bi be gay trtfdc, luc nao 
cung kem theo bong gan vung xtfdng hop - nem va xtfdng ban chan V, IV, III, 
day xtfdng ban II la khoa ngam.
Gay nhieu xtfdng ban cung mot luc thtfdng do chan thtfdng trtfc tiep nhtf 
vat nang rdi de len ban chan, xe can ngang mu ban chan hoac nga ttf cao co 
chan gap ltfng, diem cham chiu tren dau cac xtfdng ban trtfdc tien (luc tai 
nan benh nhan di chan tran hoac di giay de mem). Loai gay nay kem theo 
xep mat ltfng cac xtfdng thuyen, hop, nem.
233


2. Gay xifdng sen, xufofng got do chan thufdng nang:
Thifdng do nga tif cao, ban chan cham dat trifdc (xem cd sinh hoc 
ban chan).
Gay kin xifdng sen, got con tim thay trong trifdng hdp ngifdi ngoi trong 
xe tang bi can phai min chong tang do sifc doi tif difdi len got co chan.
C. TRIEU CHUNG
1. Gay xifdng ban chan-ngon chan
Cac xifdng nay gay co the sd nin trifc tiep o gay mot cach nhe nhang doc 
theo cac xifdng.
-  Trifdng hdp sifng ne ldn vi chan thifdng, cd the phat hien difdc mot 
cach keo nhe va don ep khe xifdng ban theo chieu doc tifng ngon 
chan mot, dau choi diem xifdng gay.
-  Trifdng hdp gay xifdng nem, xifdng hop: 15m long ban chan binh 
thifdng, kem bong gan nen mau bam tim lan xuong difdi ban chan 
gay bien dang.
2. Gay xifdng hop va xifdng nem
Cac xifdng nay thuoc co9 chan deu la xifdng ngan xop. Xung quanh lai cd 
nhieu xifdng ldn nen cac gay xifdng nay la hau qua kem theo cac gay xifdng 
ban hoac bong gan do 3. Cac gay nep nay thifdng d mat lifng ban chan nen cd 
trieu chifng dau sUng, bam tim va go manh xUdng d mu ban chan. Keo va 
don ep cac ngon chan gay dau tai cho gay.
X quang cho thay di lech (phan ldn cac xUdng nay ft di lech).
3. Gay xifdng thuyen
Xifdng thuyen nim giiJa xifdng sen va cac xifdng nem, hop, ndi cii dong 
chuyen tiep tif cac xifdng ban qua xifdng nem, hop den cac xifdng co dinh d 
goc ban chan. Xifdng thuyen la xifdng ban le, nen cd cd che gay ngUdc lai vdi 
cac xifdng trifdc sau no.
234


Cd che gay thtfdng la nuta ban chan trtfdc bi be gap long qua mtfc dot 
ngot, thtfdng di lech xa ve mat long - day chlng mat ltfng ban chan. Gay 
khong di lech xtfdng thuyen co trieu chtfng ddn gian: dau, stfng, bam, go 
xtfdng tai cho.
Can X quang kiem chtfng.
Trtfdng hdp gay xtfdng thuyen di lech-nhieu thi chen ep mach mau mu 
ban chan gay hoai tii da ltfng ban chan phfa trtfdc nen phai dtfdc nhanh 
chong nin trat gay xtfdng thuyen. Them vao dd cac ngon chan bi co rut ve 
mat ltfng khong cii dong dudi ngon chan dtfdc.
4. Gay xtfdng sen
Gay xtfdng sen luc nao cung kem theo long khdp co chan ttfdng ttf gay 
hai mat ca.
Cd che gay (xem cau true va cd sinh hoc ban chan).
Xtfdng sen gay hay trat deu cd the sd nin dtfdc qua ldp da va gan cd 
vung co chan ke ca khi stfng hay bien dang. Stf bien dang qua mtfc bat 
thtfdng la lung cua vung co’ chan can nhd tdi to’n thtfdng xtfdng sen.
a. Trieu chting
-  
Co chan rong be ngang.
-  
Stfng ne.
-  XtfOng sen sd thay qua ldp da ne.
-  X quang: kiem chtfng.
b. Bien chting
-  
Chen ep than kinh mach mau vung co’ chan gay hoai ttf phfa xa cua 
ban chan ttfc thi.
-  
Hoai tii thieu mau nudi cua chmh xtfdng sen ve sau dieu tri gay 
xtfdng sen thtfdng gap.
c. Phan loai
-  
Gay mot phan cua dau hoac than sen (kieu Sheper) hoac vom sen 
(kieu Kappis).
235


-  Gay hoan toan than xiidng sen, di gay bien chiing hoai tti xiidng sen.
Loai nay chia thanh 4 nhom:
+ 
Gay it hoac khong di lech (hoai tti 12,5%).
+ 
Gay va trat diidi sen, xiidng chay vln dinh vdi xUdng sen hoai tii 
(hoai tii 56,8%).
+ 
Gay xiidng sen va trat ban ra khoi gong kim va gay xiidng got 
(hoai tii 78,8%).
+ Gay nat nhieu manh xiidng sen.
5. Gay xiidng got
Xudng got la diem cham, diem chiu siic doi cua chan thu’dng nga tii cao, 
no min (ngoi trong xe tang) vdi co chan gap liing hay duoi, diem ttia duy 
nhat phia sau cua vong tam giac, chan de thang bang cua con ngUdi trong di 
diing, chay, nhay, rdi tii tren cao xuong (nhay du). Vi cd che gay xiidng got 
de anh hiidng den noi tang nen can tham kham ki va phat hien nhiing dau 
hieu: tran khf mang pho’i, vd tang dac, vd bang quang, vd tang rong, gay cot 
song liing, thit liing - trat kh6p hang, vd xiidng chau, dtit day chlng cheo 
khdp goi.
a. Trieu chiing vd xiidng got ddn thuan
-  
Co chan khong rong (neu m lt ca khong ton thiidng day chlng).
-  
Chieu cao tii mat ca den da ban chan ngln lai.
-  
Dau, bam tfm dii6i m lt ca (dau khi an ben than xiidng got).
-  
Bam lan canh bii6m long ban chan muon, khong gay dau long 
ban chan.
b. Phan loai
-  
Gay ngoai doi got co tien liidng tot.
-  
Gay doi got, co tien liidng xau hdn.
+ 
Gay doi got ddn gian: co tien liidng tot hdn loai sau.
+ 
Gay doi got co lun: co tien liidng tuy theo do lun.
Do 1: goc Bohler giam ft (25-30°).
Do 2: goc Bohler gan 0°.
Do 3: doi got lun hln trong xiidng got hoac vd nat.
236


D. BIEUTR!
Nen cho ngu, gay me hoac te tuy song de nin xifdng, hdn nufa phai cham 
soc da ban chan that sach trifdc khi bat dong.
1. Gay xifdng ban, xifdng hop, xifdng nem
Tuy cac xifdng ban khac cau true giai phau hoc vdi xifdng mem, nhifng 
cac kieu gay xifdng ban khdng di lech dieu tri giong nhif nhau.
Hinh 101. PhtfOng phap co dinh gay xtfdng ban chan
Can dieu tri theo Y hoc hien dai cac gay xUdng ban - nhat la khi cac 
xifdng ay cd di lech mac dau da nan.
-  
Cho cac gay xifdng ban hoac xifdng ban ke tiep nhau.
-  Gay chom cac xUdng ban.
-  Xudng ngon chan cai.
Cdn cac gay xifdng ngon chan khac thi chi can nan chinh lai roi bang kim 
giufa hai ngon lanh vdi nhau trong 3 - 6 tuan. Benh nhan phai co" gang tranh 
di ty len cac ngon chan gay trong thdi gian bat dong.
2. Dieu tri gay xifdng thuyen
Xifdng thuyen la xifdng ban le can du'dc nin gay xu'dng ngay de tranh 
hau qua chen ep mach mau, hoai tii da mat lifng ban chan trong cap ciiu.
Sau dd, tai Trung tam dieu tri chuyen khoa se dat van de ket hdp xifdng 
va phuc hdi day chang mu ban chan cua xu'dng vdi cac xu'dng xung quanh 
nhat la ddi vdi xifdng sen.
237


Sau mo, chung ta cung phai lam bot clng chan de di ngay sau mo 3 
tuan. Bot khong can day lam, nhUng diem ty van tren got.
3. Dieu tri gay xu’dng sen
Ngoai trti vai trtfdng hop gay mot phan vom than hoac co xtfOng sen 
khong di lech danh cho dieu tri bao ton co ldi, con lai tat ca trtfdng hdp gay 
xtfdng sen can ket hdp xtfdng cang sdm cang tot. Xtfdng sen gay kem trat 
khdp thi chic chin ty le hoai tii cao, nen co nhieu tac gia khuyen chung ta 
lay bo xtfdng sen hoac dong khdp co chan la thuan ldi hdn ca.
MOT SO TRAT KH6p THUONG GAP
Trat khdp co the xay ra d cac khdp: vai, khuyu, hang nhtfng trat khdp 
vai hay gap hdn.
Trieu chiing chung:
Cd nang: dau vung khdp bi trat, mat cd nang va dau hieu quan trong 
nhat la "dau hieu lo xo", nghia la khi dtfa phan ngoai vi khdp trat sang vi tri 
khac, tha ra lai trd ve vi tri cu.
Trat khdp vai:
Hau het cac trtfdng hdp trat khdp vai deu di lech chom ra trtfdc va 
xuong dtfdi. Cd the minh hpa ba loai sau day:
Hinh 102. Trat khdp vai va cac kieu di lech cua chom 
(1) Xuong dudi; (2) Tri/dc-dudi; (3) Trudc-trong.
238


PhUdng phap nan chinh:
Hinh 104. Trat khdp vai, chom di lech ra trifdc.
